# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="fc287-102">Устаревшие члены в .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fc287-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fc287-103">В этой статье перечислены члены типов, устаревшие в .NET Framework 4.5 и выше.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fc287-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fc287-104">Члены типа группируются по сборкам.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fc287-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fc287-105">В этой статье не перечисляются члены устаревших типов.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fc287-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fc287-106">См. [список устаревших типов](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fc287-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
